{"type":"assistant.message","data":{"messageId":"994b26c5-6c43-4906-9f65-dc3b8e299317","content":"Planning-only architectural assessment for “saved shapes should be draggable without selecting first”, grounded in current boundaries in [src/app/components/map/map.component.ts](src/app/components/map/map.component.ts), [src/app/services/draw-tool.service.ts](src/app/services/draw-tool.service.ts), [src/app/services/saved-shapes.service.ts](src/app/services/saved-shapes.service.ts), and [src/app/services/edit-shape-facade.service.ts](src/app/services/edit-shape-facade.service.ts).\n\n**1. Architecture Constraints And Principles**\n1. Single owner of pointer intent arbitration: keep raw Cesium pointer events centralized in one interaction layer, then dispatch semantic intents (select, drag-start, drag-update, drag-end, context-menu).  \n2. Preserve service boundaries:  \n- Map component remains orchestration/UI shell only.  \n- Draw tool remains temporary/edit geometry engine.  \n- Saved shapes service remains persisted-entity registry and mutation API.  \n- Edit facade remains form source of truth only when shape is in edit context.  \n3. Selection and drag are different concerns: dragging without pre-selection should not require explicit prior selection event; drag-start may implicitly set active shape for UX feedback.  \n4. ID-based consistency rule must stay intact: form sync only when dragged shape id equals form shape id; otherwise persisted shape update path only (no form mutation).  \n5. Event conflict minimization: avoid multiple handlers independently acting on the same left-click/down/up lifecycle without a shared decision contract.  \n6. Deterministic hit policy: hit entities remain pick target for thin lines/polygons; behavior must be shape-type agnostic.  \n7. Backward compatibility: right-click context menu behavior and existing edit-mode gate should stay unchanged unless explicitly redefined.  \n8. Failure-safe drag lifecycle: every drag-start must end in commit or rollback path, even on pointer cancellation/out-of-canvas.\n\n**2. Recommended Event/State Flow**\n1. Preconditions: edit mode enabled.  \n2. Pointer down on map: interaction coordinator resolves nearest draggable saved shape via direct pick first, then tolerance fallback.  \n3. If no shape hit: continue with current behavior (selection clear / draw flow).  \n4. If shape hit: create DragSession with shapeId, shapeType, start world position, and snapshot of original geometry.  \n5. Drag threshold gate: only after movement exceeds threshold do we enter Dragging state. This prevents accidental drags on clicks.  \n6. On threshold crossing:  \n- Implicitly mark this shape as active/selected for visual affordance.  \n- Emit drag-start semantic event.  \n7. Pointer move while dragging: update in-memory geometry for that saved shape using saved-shapes service mutation method (preview update).  \n8. Sync branch decision on each move or at drag-end:  \n- If formShapeId equals draggedShapeId: sync form through edit facade helper.  \n- Else: do not touch form; track pending persisted geometry for save/update flow.  \n9. Pointer up: commit geometry update via API orchestration path, then refresh saved entity snapshot.  \n10. On API failure: rollback to DragSession original geometry and emit user-visible error state.  \n11. Context menu/right-click path remains independent and unchanged.\n\nSuggested state model:\n- Idle  \n- PointerDownCandidate  \n- DraggingSavedShape  \n- CommitPending  \n- RollbackOnError\n\n**3. Coupling Risks And How To Avoid Them**\n1. Risk: dual handler race between map component and draw tool both listening to left-click families.  \nMitigation: introduce a single interaction coordinator service (or a strict handler priority contract) that decides ownership per pointer sequence.\n2. Risk: draw tool starts absorbing saved-shape persistence logic.  \nMitigation: keep draw tool focused on temp/edit geometry only; saved-shape drag mutation and persistence stay in saved-shapes plus API orchestration layer.\n3. Risk: form corruption when dragging non-opened saved shapes.  \nMitigation: enforce id-match guard in one shared policy function used by all drag paths.\n4. Risk: hidden business rules spread across component methods.  \nMitigation: move drag policy into an interaction policy module/service with explicit methods like canStartSavedDrag, shouldSyncForm, shouldAutoPersist.\n5. Risk: brittle Cesium entity identity assumptions (vertex/hit/main entity confusion).  \nMitigation: normalize picked entity to canonical parent shape id before any state transition.\n6. Risk: optimistic updates without rollback discipline.  \nMitigation: mandatory drag snapshot object and rollback path on network failure/timeouts.\n\n**4. Observability And Logging Expectations**\n1. Structured event logs for drag lifecycle with correlationId: drag_start, drag_move_sampled, drag_commit, drag_rollback, drag_error.  \n2. Required fields: shapeId, shapeType, formShapeId, syncMode (form-sync or persisted-only), editMode, pointerDevice, durationMs, moveCount, distanceMeters.  \n3. Sampling strategy: log all starts/ends/errors; sample move logs (for example every N moves) to avoid noise.  \n4. Business counters:  \n- drag_start_total by shape type  \n- drag_commit_success_total  \n- drag_commit_failure_total  \n- drag_without_preselect_total  \n- drag_form_sync_total versus drag_persist_only_total  \n5. UX diagnostics: threshold-cancel count (pointer down but no drag), rollback count, and median drag latency from start to commit.  \n6. Error policy: user-facing message on commit failure plus developer log with rollback result and sanitized API error payload.\n\n**5. Minimal Vertical Slice Plan (Small Tasks, Dependencies, Acceptance Criteria)**\n1. Task VS-01: Define interaction contract and state machine  \nDepends on: none  \nAcceptance criteria: documented state transitions and ownership table approved; explicit policy for click versus drag threshold and id-based sync branching.\n2. Task VS-02: Add interaction coordinator skeleton (no behavior change yet)  \nDepends on: VS-01  \nAcceptance criteria: existing selection and context menu flows still pass; coordinator receives pointer events and emits no-op semantic events.\n3. Task VS-03: Implement drag-start without pre-selection detection for saved shapes  \nDepends on: VS-02  \nAcceptance criteria: in edit mode, pointer down plus move on a saved shape starts drag even when not previously selected; plain click without move still behaves as click/selection.\n4. Task VS-04: Implement live geometry preview updates for saved shapes during drag  \nDepends on: VS-03  \nAcceptance criteria: polyline/polygon/circle/text saved shapes visibly move while dragging; thin-shape hit behavior remains reliable.\n5. Task VS-05: Implement commit and rollback persistence path  \nDepends on: VS-04  \nAcceptance criteria: successful drag persists via API and refreshes saved snapshot; failed persistence restores original geometry and shows error feedback.\n6. Task VS-06: Implement form-sync policy guard  \nDepends on: VS-05  \nAcceptance criteria: form updates only when dragged shape id equals current form shape id; otherwise form remains unchanged while saved entity updates.\n7. Task VS-07: Add observability instrumentation  \nDepends on: VS-03, VS-05, VS-06  \nAcceptance criteria: lifecycle logs and counters emitted with required fields; failure and rollback are traceable with one correlation id.\n8. Task VS-08: Focused verification pack  \nDepends on: VS-03 through VS-07  \nAcceptance criteria:  \n- Unit tests for state transitions, id-guard policy, rollback behavior.  \n- Component/service integration tests for coordinator-to-service calls.  \n- E2E scenarios: drag without preselect, click-only no-drag, API failure rollback, edit-opened shape form sync, non-opened shape no form sync.\n\nIf you want, I can next produce a one-page sequence diagram and a responsibility matrix (component/service by event) as implementation-ready architecture artifacts.","toolRequests":[],"reasoningText":""},"id":"066efaa9-fdfd-4869-a73a-1397fc33e536","timestamp":"2026-05-27T06:38:46.665Z","parentId":"6f800108-482c-425a-8f0e-d594f39b9770"}

this.suppressNextLeftClick = true;\n      this.savedShapesService.selectShape(this.dragSession.shapeId);\n    }\n\n    const delta = Cartesian3.subtract(\n      currentAnchor,\n      this.dragSession.lastDragCartesian,\n      new Cartesian3(),\n    );\n\n    const draggedShape = this.savedShapesService.getShapeById(\n      this.dragSession.shapeId,\n    );\n    const sourceDto = draggedShape?.shapeDto ?? this.dragSession.latestDto;\n    const translated = this.translateShapeDtoByDelta(sourceDto, delta);\n    this.savedShapesService.updateShape(translated);\n\n    this.dragSession.latestDto = translated;\n    this.dragSession.lastDragCartesian = currentAnchor;\n  }\n\n  finishDrag(): void {\n    const session = this.dragSession;\n    this.dragSession = null;\n\n    if (!session?.hasDragged) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    this.shapeApiService.update(session.shapeId, session.latestDto).subscribe({\n      next: (savedShape) => {\n        this.savedShapesService.updateShape(savedShape);\n      },\n      error: (error) => {\n        this.savedShapesService.updateShape(session.originalDto);\n        console.error('Error saving dragged shape:', error);\n        if (\n          typeof window !== 'undefined' &&\n          typeof window.alert === 'function'\n        ) {\n          window.alert('Unable to save dragged shape. Position was restored.');\n        }\n      },\n    });\n  }\n\n  consumeSuppressedLeftClick(): boolean {\n    if (!this.suppressNextLeftClick) {\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    this.suppressNextLeftClick = false;\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  resetDragState(): void {\n    this.dragSession = null;\n    this.suppressNextLeftClick = false;\n  }\n\n  private pickSavedShapeTarget(viewer: Viewer | null, position: Cartesian2) {\n    try {\n      return viewer?.scene.pick(position);\n    } catch {\n      return undefined;\n    }\n  }\n\n  private pickMapPosition(viewer: Viewer, position: Cartesian2): Cartesian3 | null {\n    let cartesian = viewer.camera.pickEllipsoid(\n      position,\n      viewer.scene.globe.ellipsoid,\n    );\n\n    if (!cartesian) {\n      const ray = viewer.scene.camera.getPickRay(position);\n      if (!ray) {\n        return null;\n      }\n      cartesian = viewer.scene.globe.pick(ray, viewer.scene);\n    }\n\n    return cartesian ?? null;\n  }\n\n  private translateShapeDtoByDelta(shape: ShapeDto, delta: Cartesian3): ShapeDto {\n    const translatedPoints = shape.points.map((point) => {\n      const originalCartesian = Cartesian3.fromDegrees(\n        point.coordinates.longitude,\n        point.coordinates.latitude,\n        (point.altitude?.feet ?? 0) / FEET_PER_METER,\n      );\n      const translatedCartesian = Cartesian3.add(\n        originalCartesian,\n        delta,\n        new Cartesian3(),\n      );\n      const translatedCartographic = Cartographic.fromCartesian(translatedCartesian);\n\n      return {\n        coordinates: {\n          latitude: CesiumMath.toDegrees(translatedCartographic.latitude),\n          longitude: CesiumMath.toDegrees(translatedCartographic.longitude),\n        },\n        altitude: {\n          feet: translatedCartographic.height * FEET_PER_METER,\n        },\n      };\n    });\n\n    return {\n      ...shape,\n      points: translatedPoints,\n    };\n  }\n\n  private cloneShapeDto(shape: ShapeDto): ShapeDto {\n    return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shape)) as ShapeDto;\n  }\n}\n"}},"id":"b117cb2c-6c3a-42e6-843e-46bfeb36e78c","timestamp":"2026-05-27T07:13:22.566Z","parentId":"9b3270eb-02b3-49c8-af24-da4f0bf7619b"}
